In a hotel that costs more than 2,700 a night, room service is called from 5:00 p.m. to 9:30 p.m., and no aunt comes, not even a bottle of water. The aunt came and put down the towel and left without looking at the trash can to see if there was something missing. I called again before helping to take out the garbage and clean up the room. I just want to ask, what good service and good living environment can cost 2700 a night? Is it the capital provided by the underground parking lot with cement floor, cement wall and soil on the ground?
